The ranking of the cards in this deck are as follows (from high to low); Ace, King, Queen, Jack, 10, 9, 8, 7, 6, 5, 4, 3, 2. \r\n\r\nThe player who draws the highest card of all would be designated the first dealer. \r\n\r\nThe dealer shuffles the cards and deals the hand.
